// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/sfxtextures_sfx_blocks17g_jumpad_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/sfx/blocks17g_jumpad
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_blocks17g_jumpad;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_lightmap;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_bouncepad01b_layer1;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;
// stage3's externs
uniform texture stage3_;
uniform float3x2 stage3_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_blocks17g_jumpad>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_bouncepad01b_layer1>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage3_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage3_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};
struct stage3_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD3;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
	stage3_input stage3;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage3.uv = input.texcoords;
	// Invalid or unparsed tcMod statement.

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_blocks17g_jumpad
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	// stage2_bouncepad01b_layer1
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage3_
	destination = (tex2D(stage3_sampler, input.stage3.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_proto_zzztblu;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;
// stage3's externs
uniform texture stage3_spawn_floord2c;
uniform float3x2 stage3_tcmod;
// stage4's externs
uniform texture stage4_lightmap;
uniform float3x2 stage4_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_proto_zzztblu>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage3_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage3_spawn_floord2c>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage4_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage4_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};
struct stage3_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD3;
};
struct stage4_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD4;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
	stage3_input stage3;
	stage4_input stage4;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (5.6 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (5.6 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 0.5;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 0.5;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.x;
	 float t_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.y;
	output.stage1.uv.x = s_stage1*cos(2.268928 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * -sin(2.268928 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(2.268928 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(2.268928 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.y = s_stage1*sin(2.268928 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * cos(2.268928 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(2.268928 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(2.268928 * gameTime));
	// Invalid or unparsed tcMod statement.
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.x;
	 float t_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.y;
	output.stage2.uv.x = s_stage2*cos(1.396263 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * -sin(1.396263 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(1.396263 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(1.396263 * gameTime));
	output.stage2.uv.y = s_stage2*sin(1.396263 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * cos(1.396263 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(1.396263 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(1.396263 * gameTime));
	// Invalid or unparsed tcMod statement.
	output.stage3.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage4.uv = input.lightmapcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_proto_zzztblu
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	// stage2_
	float4 stage2_source = tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv);
	destination = (stage2_source * stage2_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage2_source.a));

	// stage3_spawn_floord2c
	float4 stage3_source = tex2D(stage3_sampler, input.stage3.uv);
	destination = (stage3_source * stage3_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage3_source.a));

	// stage4_lightmap
	destination = (tex2D(stage4_sampler, input.stage4.uv) * destination) + (destination * (1.0 -destination.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

	 float s_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.x;
	 float t_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.y;
	output.stage2.uv.x = s_stage2*cos(1.396263 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * -sin(1.396263 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(1.396263 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(1.396263 * gameTime));
	output.stage2.uv.y = s_stage2*sin(1.396263 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * cos(1.396263 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(1.396263 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(1.396263 * gameTime));
	// Invalid or unparsed tcMod statement.
	output.stage3.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage4.uv = input.lightmapcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_firegorre2
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	// stage2_
	float4 stage2_source = tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv);
	destination = (stage2_source * stage2_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage2_source.a));

	// stage3_spawn_floor
	float4 stage3_source = tex2D(stage3_sampler, input.stage3.uv);
	destination = (stage3_source * stage3_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage3_source.a));

	// stage4_lightmap
	destination = (tex2D(stage4_sampler, input.stage4.uv) * destination) + (destination * (1.0 -destination.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

{

	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (1.6 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (1.6 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.25;

	output.stage0.uv.y *= 0.5;

	 float t_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.y;

	 float s_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.x;
	 float t_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.y;
	output.stage2.uv.x = s_stage2*cos(1.396263 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * -sin(1.396263 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(1.396263 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(1.396263 * gameTime));
	output.stage2.uv.y = s_stage2*sin(1.396263 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * cos(1.396263 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(1.396263 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(1.396263 * gameTime));

	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_metalfloor_wall_14b
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	// stage2_metalfloor_wall_14bglow
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;

{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 2.857143;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 2.857143;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.07 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.015;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.07 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.015;
	// Invalid or unparsed tcMod statement.
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 2;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 2;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.03 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.025;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.03 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.025;
	// Invalid or unparsed tcMod statement.

	return output;
};

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/sfxtextures_sfx_glass_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/sfx/glass
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_lightmap;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_oldwindow;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_lightmap;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_oldwindow>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 4;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 4;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.lightmapcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_lightmap
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage1_oldwindow
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * (1.0 -stage1_source.a)) + (destination * stage1_source.a);

	// stage2_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv) * destination;

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/sfxtextures_sfx_fan_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/sfx/fan
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_lightmap;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(4.468043 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(4.468043 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(4.468043 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(4.468043 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(4.468043 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(4.468043 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(4.468043 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(4.468043 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv = input.lightmapcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(4.468043 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(4.468043 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(4.468043 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(4.468043 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(4.468043 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(4.468043 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(4.468043 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(4.468043 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv = input.lightmapcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_
	float4 stage0_source = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);
	destination = (stage0_source * stage0_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage0_source.a));

	// stage1_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(4.468043 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(4.468043 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(4.468043 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(4.468043 * gameTime));

	return destination;

// Shader: textures/sfx/zap_scroll1000
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_zap_scroll;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_zap_scroll;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_zap_scroll2;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;
// stage3's externs
uniform texture stage3_zap_scroll2;
uniform float3x2 stage3_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_zap_scroll>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_zap_scroll>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_zap_scroll2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage3_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage3_zap_scroll2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};
struct stage3_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD3;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
	stage3_input stage3;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= -1;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 1;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv.x *= -1;
	output.stage2.uv.y *= 1;
	output.stage2.uv.x += 2 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage3.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage3.uv.x += -1.3 * gameTime;
	output.stage3.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_zap_scroll
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage1_zap_scroll
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage2_zap_scroll2
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage3_zap_scroll2
	destination = (tex2D(stage3_sampler, input.stage3.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	{

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/sfxtextures_sfx_swirl_r1_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/sfx/swirl_r1
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(-3.281219 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(-3.281219 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(-3.281219 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(-3.281219 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(-3.281219 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(-3.281219 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(-3.281219 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(-3.281219 * gameTime));

	stage1_input stage1;

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{

	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 1;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 2.5;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 0.3 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= -1;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 5;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 0.3 * gameTime;

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_metalfloor_wall_15glass
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv) * float4(1.0 - destination.r, 1.0 - destination.g, 1.0 - destination.b, 1.0 - destination.a);

	// stage1_metalfloor_wall_15glass
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/sfxtextures_sfx_portal_sfx_ring_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/sfx/portal_sfx_ring
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_portal_sfx_ring_blue1;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_portal_sfx_ring_electric;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_portal_sfx1;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;
// stage3's externs
uniform texture stage3_portal_sfx_ring;
uniform float3x2 stage3_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_portal_sfx_ring_blue1>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_portal_sfx_ring_electric>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_portal_sfx1>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage3_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage3_portal_sfx_ring>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};
struct stage3_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD3;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
	stage3_input stage3;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 0.5 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.x;
	 float t_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.y;
	output.stage2.uv.x = s_stage2*cos(6.283185 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * -sin(6.283185 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(6.283185 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(6.283185 * gameTime));
	output.stage2.uv.y = s_stage2*sin(6.283185 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * cos(6.283185 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(6.283185 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(6.283185 * gameTime));
	output.stage3.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_portal_sfx_ring_blue1
	float4 stage0_source = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);
	destination = (stage0_source * stage0_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage0_source.a));

	// stage1_portal_sfx_ring_electric
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage2_portal_sfx1
	destination = tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv) * destination;

	// stage3_portal_sfx_ring
	destination = (tex2D(stage3_sampler, input.stage3.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/sfxtextures_sfx_grid_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/sfx/grid
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_grid;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_grid>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_grid
	float4 stage0_source = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);
	destination = (stage0_source * stage0_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage0_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;

sampler stage3_sampler = sampler_state

	Texture = <stage3_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};
struct stage3_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD3;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
	stage3_input stage3;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage3.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage3.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage3.uv.y += 2 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_launchpad_diamond
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	// stage2_launchpad_dot
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage3_
	destination = (tex2D(stage3_sampler, input.stage3.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	stage3_input stage3;

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage3.uv = input.texcoords;
	// Invalid or unparsed tcMod statement.

	return output;

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_bounce_largeblock3b
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	// stage2_bouncepad01b_layer1
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage3_
	destination = (tex2D(stage3_sampler, input.stage3.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/sfxtextures_sfx_goopq1metal7_98d_pent_256_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/sfx/goopq1metal7_98d_pent_256
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_goopq1metal7_98d;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_pentfloor_256;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_goopq1metal7_98d>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_pentfloor_256>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_goopq1metal7_98d
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_pentfloor_256
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_lightmap;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_pitted_rust3;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_orangestripes;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_pitted_rust3>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_orangestripes>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_pitted_rust3
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	// stage2_orangestripes
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/sfxtextures_sfx_pentagramfloor_rotating_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/sfx/pentagramfloor_rotating
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_lightmap;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_xhugefloor2;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_xhugefloor2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.x;
	 float t_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.y;
	output.stage2.uv.x = s_stage2*cos(-1.047198 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * -sin(-1.047198 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(-1.047198 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(-1.047198 * gameTime));
	output.stage2.uv.y = s_stage2*sin(-1.047198 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * cos(-1.047198 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(-1.047198 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(-1.047198 * gameTime));

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_xhugefloor2
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	// stage2_
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;

};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_q1met_redpad
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	// stage2_q1met_redpad_blend
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/sfxtextures_sfx_xfiretest1_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/sfx/xfiretest1
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_firetestb;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_firetest;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_firetest2;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_firetestb>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_firetest>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_firetest2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.2;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.2;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 4;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 4;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0.5 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1.5 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 10;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 10;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.5 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage2.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.5 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage2.uv.x += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv.y += 5 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_firetestb
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_firetest
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination) + (destination * tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv).a);

	// stage2_firetest2
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv) * destination) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;

	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.5 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.5 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.25;

	return output;
};

	// stage0_powerupshit

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;

	AddressV = Wrap;

	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;

	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.x;
	 float t_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.y;
	output.stage2.uv.x = s_stage2*cos(-1.047198 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * -sin(-1.047198 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(-1.047198 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(-1.047198 * gameTime));
	output.stage2.uv.y = s_stage2*sin(-1.047198 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * cos(-1.047198 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(-1.047198 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(-1.047198 * gameTime));

	return output;
};

	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.2;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.2;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 4;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 4;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0.5 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1.5 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 10;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 10;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.5 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage2.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.5 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage2.uv.x += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv.y += 5 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_firetestb
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_firetest
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination) + (destination * tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv).a);

	// stage2_firetest2
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv) * destination) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	output.stage1.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 10;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 10;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.5 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage2.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.5 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage2.uv.x += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv.y += 5 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_firetestb
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_firetest
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination) + (destination * tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv).a);

	// stage2_firetest2
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv) * destination) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/sfxtextures_sfx_teslacoil_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/sfx/teslacoil
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_lightmap;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_tesla1;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_electricslime;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;
// stage3's externs
uniform texture stage3_cabletest2;
uniform float3x2 stage3_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_tesla1>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_electricslime>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage3_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage3_cabletest2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};
struct stage3_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD3;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
	stage3_input stage3;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 1;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 2;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage1.uv.x += -1 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += -1 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv.x *= 2;
	output.stage2.uv.y *= 2;
	output.stage2.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	output.stage2.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.1;
	 float s_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.x;
	 float t_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.y;
	output.stage2.uv.x = s_stage2*cos(3.141593 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * -sin(3.141593 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(3.141593 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(3.141593 * gameTime));
	output.stage2.uv.y = s_stage2*sin(3.141593 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * cos(3.141593 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(3.141593 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(3.141593 * gameTime));
	output.stage2.uv.x += -1 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv.y += -1 * gameTime;
	output.stage3.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv) * destination;

	// stage1_tesla1
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage2_electricslime
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage3_cabletest2
	float4 stage3_source = tex2D(stage3_sampler, input.stage3.uv);
	destination = (stage3_source * stage3_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage3_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	minfilter = LINEAR;

	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_q1metal7_98d_pent_256
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	// stage2_pentagramfloor_256x256
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;

	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;

	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;

	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= -20;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= -20;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0.01 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += -0.01 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 20;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 20;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 0.01 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += -0.01 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_kc_fogcloud3
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv) * destination;

	// stage1_kc_fogcloud3
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

	AddressV = Wrap;

{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input

	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_pitted_rust3arrow
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	// stage2_pitted_rust3arrow_blend
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/sfxtextures_sfx_q1teleporter_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/sfx/q1teleporter
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_q1teleporter;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_q1teleporter>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.2 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.3;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.2 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.3;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_q1teleporter
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= -20;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= -20;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0.01 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += -0.01 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 20;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 20;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 0.01 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += -0.01 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_kc_fogcloud3
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv) * destination;

	// stage1_kc_fogcloud3
	destination = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination;

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/sfxtextures_sfx_bugmirror_generated.fx
// Shader: textures/sfx/bugmirror
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_mirror1;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_mirrorkc;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_mirror1>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_mirrorkc>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_mirror1
	float4 stage0_source = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);
	destination = (stage0_source) + (destination * (1.0 -stage0_source.a));

	// stage1_mirrorkc
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}
